 ' saal 2012 main badi sankhya main shraddhaluon kii maut par supreme court kii chintaa ke baad gathit visheshgy samiti ne sheethal peya padaarthon or tale bhune junk food ke khaane ke prati chetaya tha, kyonki amarnath gupha ke raste main oxigen kii kami hoti he
 The comments anand ne kaha, ‚Äòswasthya visheshgyon kaa kahana he ki paryaapt oxigen kii aapurti ke abhaav main aise khaadya padaarthon ko pachaana mushkil ho jaataa he, jisase saans lene main dikkat hone lagati he or shraddhaluon ke liye yatra kathin ho jaati he
